<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспечный.html>беспе́чный</a> (11666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">печ(<a href = vnd.unilang:аль.html>а́ль</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peč(álʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспечный.html>беспе́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bespéčnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)беспе́чнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)беспе́чней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>careless, carefree, unconcerned</li>
<li>nonchalant</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бес.html>бес</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пе́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>беспе́чнее, беспе́чней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-беспечн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бес.html>бес</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пе́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.

***бесподобный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бесподобный.html>бесподо́бный</a> (24836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1789. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подобный.html>подо́бный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podóbnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly, a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">incomparable</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бесподобный.html>бесподо́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bespodóbnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>peerless, incomparable, matchless</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бесподо́бность</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bespodóbnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***беспокоить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоить.html>беспоко́ить</a> (3667)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bez</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pokojь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоить.html>беспоко́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bespokóitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побеспокоить.html>побеспоко́ить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обеспокоить.html>обеспоко́ить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bother, to disturb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоить.html>беспоко́ить</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne xočú tebjá <b>bespokóitʹ</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't want to bother you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досаждать.html>досажда́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dosaždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешать.html>меша́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волновать.html>волнова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">volnovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">trevóžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоиться.html>беспоко́иться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bespokóitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забеспокоиться.html>забеспоко́иться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zabespokóitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обеспокоить.html>обеспоко́ить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obespokóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побеспокоить.html>побеспоко́ить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobespokóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бес.html>бес</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ить</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:обеспокоить.html>обеспоко́ить</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:побеспокоить.html>побеспоко́ить</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>бес-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-покоj-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***беспокоиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоиться.html>беспоко́иться</a> (2473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоить.html>беспоко́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bespokóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоиться.html>беспоко́иться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bespokóitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">побеспоко́иться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забеспокоиться.html>забеспоко́иться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обеспоко́иться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to worry (about)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоиться.html>беспоко́иться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> ко́м-либо/чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bespokóitʹsja</b> o kóm-libo/čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to worry about someone/something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be anxious (about), to be uneasy (about)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоить.html>беспоко́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bespokóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***беспокойный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойный.html>беспоко́йный</a> (8237)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоить.html>беспоко́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bespokóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойный.html>беспоко́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bespokójnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>uneasy, restive, anxious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойный.html>беспоко́йный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгляд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bespokójnyj</b> vzgljad</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>troubled</b> look, <b>anxious</b> look</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>disturbing</li>
<li>restless, fidgety</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоить.html>беспоко́ить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bespokóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойство.html>беспоко́йство</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bespokójstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pokój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бес.html>бес</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>ко́й</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойный.html>беспоко́йный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bespokójnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойство.html>беспоко́йство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bespokójstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойство.html>беспоко́йства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойство.html>беспоко́йства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойство.html>беспоко́йств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>anxiety, concern, uneasiness, nervousness</li>
<li>trouble</li></ol>

***бесполезный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бесполезный.html>бесполе́зный</a> (6488)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:польза.html>по́льза</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pólʹza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полезный.html>поле́зный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poléznyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for the phonological development.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бесполезный.html>бесполе́зный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bespoléznyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>useless, unavailing, vain</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспорядочный.html>беспоря́дочный</a> (11216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспорядок.html>беспоря́док</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">besporjádok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспорядочный.html>беспоря́дочный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">besporjádočnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>disorderly, confused, irregular, random
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:беспорядочный.html>беспоря́дочный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>besporjádočnyj</b> ogónʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sporadic</b> fire</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:беспорядочный.html>беспоря́дочные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:половой.html>половы́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>besporjádočnyje</b> polovýje svjázi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sexual promiscuity</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>random</b> sexual contacts</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***беспочвенный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспочвенный.html>беспочвенный</a> (30857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1874. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póčva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">grundlos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспочвенный.html>беспо́чвенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bespóčvennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>baseless, groundless <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">not grounded in facts, not based on anything true</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">безоснова́тельный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bezosnovátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>First attested in 1845. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Rechtlosigkeit</i>.

***бесправный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бесправный.html>беспра́вный</a> (27035)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">rechtlos</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бесправный.html>беспра́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">besprávnyj</span>)
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бес.html>бес</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">престан-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prestan-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on a combining stem of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">преста́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prestátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cease, to quit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare 1sg. present <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">преста́ну</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prestánu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бес.html>бес</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пря.html>пре́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>це<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>де́нт<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспризорный.html>беспризорный</a> (17861)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">призор-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prizor-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on a combining stem of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">призре́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prizrétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to support by charity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">obsolete</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зоркий.html>зо́ркий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zórkij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vigilant, watchful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зреть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zretʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to watch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
